The generic apiserver registers plugins via staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go (RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins), and the kube-apiserver adds all kube-specific plugins in pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go and configures options in pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go.\\n\\n## 2. server admission controller pipeline is implemented primarily in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/ and its subdirectories.\\n\\n## 1. admission.Interface Registration\\n\\nThe core interface is defined in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go, which declares Interface, MutationInterface, ValidationInterface, and PluginInitializer. Plugin registration is managed via the Plugins struct in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugins.go, which provides Register() to add named factory functions and NewFromPlugins() to instantiate the ordered chain. The generic apiserver registers plugins via staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go (RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins), and the kube-apiserver adds all kube-specific plugins in pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go and configures options in pkg/kubeapiserver/options/admission.go.\\n\\n## 2. Generic Admission Chain Execution\\n\\nstaging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go implements chainAdmissionHandler, which iterates over all registered handlers invoking Admit() (for MutationInterface) and then Validate() (for ValidationInterface) on each. staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/reinvocation.go wraps the chain in a reinvoker that re-invokes when webhooks request it. Metrics instrumentation is in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/metrics/metrics.go. Audit decoration is in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/audit.go. Plugin initializers are in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/initializer/ and pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/.\\n\\n## 3. Mutating Admission Ordering\\n\\nThe MutatingAdmissionWebhook plugin (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go) implements MutationInterface and uses dispatcher.go to call mutating webhooks in order, with re-invocation via reinvocationcontext.go. The CEL-based MutatingAdmissionPolicy plugin (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/mutating/plugin.go) works similarly via its dispatcher and reinvocation context. The patch sub-package handles ApplyConfiguration and JSON patch mutations. The shared generic policy infrastructure (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/generic/) is shared between mutating and validating policy plugins.\\n\\n## 4. Validating Admission Webhook Call\\n\\nThe ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugin (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go) implements ValidationInterface and calls webhooks via dispatcher.go. The CEL-based ValidatingAdmissionPolicy plugin (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/validating/plugin.go) evaluates CEL expressions. Webhook configuration is maintained live via staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/ (mutating_webhook_manager.go, validating_webhook_manager.go). Shared webhook infrastructure (request building, match conditions, accessors, etc.) lives under staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
